msg:The hotel is right next to the national highway coming out of the toll station. I thought it would be noisy, but it actually felt very good when I arrived at the hotel. It has a Southeast Asian style, and the air is filled with a light fragrance. The housekeeper service is very good. He took me into the room for a brief introduction. The room is large, designed in the Southeast Asian style, very comfortable, with a terrace, suitable for my husband to smoke but not disturb me and the children, he can also rest, and the view is very good, the air is fresh. The hotel is particularly friendly and considerate to children. Not only does it provide children with a portion of fruit, cherry tomatoes, oranges, bananas, and hot milk before bedtime, but it also provides children's slippers and children's toothbrushes. The housekeeper asked us if we needed a bath, and provided 2 disposable bathtub covers. I took my children to take a bath and play. In short, I had a great time. The children were so happy that they didn't want to come out. The bathtub and water were very good. The children were hungry, so there was a buffet on the second floor, where breakfast was also served. Generally speaking, the land of Qilu is rich in products, and the food is good. The price is very friendly, 108 per person, and children under 1.1 meters are free. The hot spring bath is only more than 40. It's a pity that the children's playground is inside the hot spring bath, and you need to pay to enter. I can only do it next time. When I checked out, they gave me a piece of fruit and a bottle of water, which doubled my favorability.

msg:I went to Europa Park Animal Kingdom and looked for a hotel for a long time. Finally, I chose Peacock King, which is in Qihe County and is very close to the Animal Kingdom in more than ten minutes! After booking with Ctrip, I received a call from the staff Ni Shasha one day in advance to confirm the check-in and add WeChat. Shasha warmly informed us of the location and weather temperature. After arriving, I went directly to the fourth floor to check in. We arrived at almost ten o'clock in the evening. At more than eight o'clock, Shasha also contacted us on WeChat to inform us that we had prepared good night milk for the children, and the precautions for dining and hot springs the next day. It was very thoughtful~
When checking in, I saw that I brought a child and gave him a high-legged car. I kept playing with it in my hands during the two days I played there. Haha, the child received a small gift and was very happy.
The room is large, warm, the light is slightly darker, there is a terrace, there is plenty of bottled water in the room, and there is a fruit plate. The oranges and tomatoes are delicious haha~
There are some shortcomings, the light is dim, the vision is inconvenient, the quilt is warm, the quilt cover is hard, and it will make noise when turning over. If you sleep lightly, it will have a little impact, but these do not affect my good impression of this hotel. The hygiene is dark, so it's hard to see clearly. There are double eyelids of the previous guest stuck on the big dressing mirror, and the rag that the lady forgot to take away after cleaning up... Oh, by the way, there are no disposable underwear in the hot spring, if you wear a swimsuit and don't bring it, you have to go in without anything ğŸ˜‚
The deepest feeling is the staff Ni Shasha's concern, good night milk, whether you got home safely, and if you have any questions, you will get a response quickly on WeChat, which is great! All five-star praise! I hope I will have the opportunity to stay in the future~
